Introduction

The API documentation for Bookshelves to use endpoints with another app.

This documentation aims to provide all the information you need to work with our API.

As you scroll, you'll see code examples for working with the API in different programming languages in the dark area to the right (or as part of the content on mobile). You can switch the language used with the tabs at the top right (or from the nav menu at the top left on mobile).

Base URL

http://localhost:8000

Authenticating requests

To authenticate requests, include an Authorization header with the value "Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}".

All authenticated endpoints are marked with a requires authentication badge in the documentation below.

You can retrieve your token by visiting your dashboard and clicking Generate API token.

Account

GET Current user.

requires authentication

Route name: api.v1.profile

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/profile" \
    --header "Authorization: Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/profile"
);

const headers = {
    "Authorization": "Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://localhost:8000/api/v1/profile',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Authorization' => 'Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}',
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

Example response (401):

Show headers 
cache-control: no-cache, private
content-type: application/json
vary: Origin
 

{
    "message": "Unauthenticated."
}

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/authors?perPage=5&page=1" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/authors"
);

const params = {
    "perPage": "5",
    "page": "1",
};
Object.keys(params)
    .forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://localhost:8000/api/v1/authors',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
        'query' => [
            'perPage'=> '5',
            'page'=> '1',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

Paru pour la premiere fois le 14 octobre 2010 avec le tome 1 \" la pale lumiere des tenebres \", elle s'acheva prematurement le 12 avril 2013 avec le tome 8 \" le regard brulant des etoiles \". En effet, le deces soudain de Pierre Bottero en novembre 2009 dans un accident de moto a oblige Erik L'Homme a terminer seul la serie. Sur les 13 tomes prevus au depart, seuls 8 sortiront. Il etait prevu , qu'ils ecriraient les tomes en alternance, par paire: Erik ecrivant le tome du point de vue de son personnage, Jasper, puis Pierre ecrit ce que vivait son personnage, Ombe, au meme moment. A la mort de Pierre, Erik prit la decision de continuer la serie avec toutefois une nuance majeure: Pierre s'etant tue en moto, ainsi mourut Ombe, laissant a Jasper le soin de continuer l'aventure seul, ou presque. As a very young man, he came to live in Provence, a region he never left since then. He said that he wouldn't be able to live without sun, mistral and cicadas.                 "description": "A comme Association est une serie de romans pour la jeunesse ecrite par Pierre Bottero et Erik L'Homme, coeditee par les editions Gallimard Jeunesse et Rageot. Paru pour la premiere fois le 14 octobre 2010 avec le tome 1 \" la pale lumiere des tenebres \", elle s'acheva prematurement le 12 avril 2013 avec le tome 8 \" le regard brulant des etoiles \". En effet, le deces soudain de Pierre Bottero en novembre 2009 dans un accident de moto a oblige Erik L'Homme a terminer seul la serie. Sur les 13 tomes prevus au depart, seuls 8 sortiront. Il etait prevu , qu'ils ecriraient les tomes en alternance, par paire: Erik ecrivant le tome du point de vue de son personnage, Jasper, puis Pierre ecrit ce que vivait son personnage, Ombe, au meme moment. A la mort de Pierre, Erik prit la decision de continuer la serie avec toutefois une nuance majeure: Pierre s'etant tue en moto, ainsi mourut Ombe, laissant a Jasper le soin de continuer l'aventure seul, ou presque. As a very young man, he came to live in Provence, a region he never left since then. He said that he wouldn't be able to live without sun, mistral and cicadas. En effet, le deces soudain de Pierre Bottero en novembre 2009 dans un accident de moto a oblige Erik L'Homme a terminer seul la serie. Sur les 13 tomes prevus au depart, seuls 8 sortiront. Il etait prevu , qu'ils ecriraient les tomes en alternance, par paire: Erik ecrivant le tome du point de vue de son personnage, Jasper, puis Pierre ecrit ce que vivait son personnage, Ombe, au meme moment. A la mort de Pierre, Erik prit la decision de continuer la serie avec toutefois une nuance majeure: Pierre s'etant tue en moto, ainsi mourut Ombe, laissant a Jasper le soin de continuer l'aventure seul, ou presque. GET api/v1/books/{author_slug}/{book_slug}

URL Parameters

author_slug  string  

slug of author in meta.author books' list, in case of multiple authors, default author is selected so you need to refer to books' list and not authors' list, example: troisi-licia

book_slug  string  

slug of book in meta.slug books' list, example: larbre-didhunn-fr

GET Book collection related entries.

WITH PAGINATION

Get all Series/Books related to selected Book from Tag/Genre.

Route name: api.v1.books.related

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/books/related/pratchett-terry/au-guet-fr?perPage=5&page=1" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/books/related/pratchett-terry/au-guet-fr"
);

const params = {
    "perPage": "5",
    "page": "1",
};
Object.keys(params)
    .forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://localhost:8000/api/v1/books/related/pratchett-terry/au-guet-fr',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
        'query' => [
            'perPage'=> '5',
            'page'=> '1',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/books/selection"
);

    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());

);

Download

Endpoint to download EPUB/ZIP.

Content-Type application/epub+zip

Download Book EPUB, find by slug of book and slug of author.

Route name: api.v1.download.book

Example request:

    --get "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/download/book/bell-jay/something-like-autumn-en" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/epub+zip" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"

Request      

GET api/v1/download/book/{author_slug}/{book_slug}

URL Parameters

author_slug  string  

slug of author in meta.author books' list, in case of multiple authors, default author is selected so you need to refer to books' list and not authors' list, example: bell-jay

book_slug  string  

slug of book in meta.slug books' list, example: something-like-autumn-en

GET api/v1/enums

GET Count.

Get count of entities for a selected collection. Available for Book, Serie and Author.

Route name: api.v1.count

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/count?entities=author%2Cbook%2Cserie&languages=fr%2Cen" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/count"
);

const params = {
    "entities": "author,book,serie",
    "languages": "fr,en",
};
Object.keys(params)
    .forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://localhost:8000/api/v1/count',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
        'query' => [
            'entities'=> 'author,book,serie',
            'languages'=> 'fr,en',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

Example response (200):

Show headers 
cache-control: no-cache, private
content-type: application/json
x-ratelimit-limit: 5000
x-ratelimit-remaining: 4981
vary: Origin
 

{
    "data": {
        "entities": {
            "author": 62,
            "book": 593,
            "serie": 85
        },
        "languages": {
            "fr": 476,
            "en": 0
        }
    }
}

POST Send submission.

Route name: api.v1.submission.send

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/submission" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"name\": \"et\",
    \"email\": \"edmund.bahringer@example.net\",
    \"honeypot\": false,
    \"message\": \"udhrvhsncdkjacl\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/submission"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "name": "et",
    "email": "edmund.bahringer@example.net",
    "honeypot": false,
    "message": "udhrvhsncdkjacl"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->post(
    'http://localhost:8000/api/v1/submission',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
        'json' => [
            'name' => 'et',
            'email' => 'edmund.bahringer@example.net',
            'honeypot' => false,
            'message' => 'udhrvhsncdkjacl',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

Example response (422):

Show headers 
cache-control: no-cache, private
content-type: application/json
x-ratelimit-limit: 5000
x-ratelimit-remaining: 4976
vary: Origin
 

{
    "message": "The email must be a valid email address.",
    "errors": {
        "email": [
            "The email must be a valid email address."
        ]
    }
}
Received response:
Request failed with error:

Must be at least 15 characters.

    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://localhost:8000/api/v1/publishers',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

Search

GET Search.

Search full-text into authors, books & series.

Route name: api.v1.search.index

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/search?q=la+communaut%C3%A9+de+l%27anneau" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/search"
);

const params = {
    "q": "la communauté de l'anneau",
};
Object.keys(params)
    .forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://localhost:8000/api/v1/search',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
        'query' => [
            'q'=> 'la communauté de l'anneau',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

GET api/v1/series

Query Parameters

To select specific lang, null by default.

Number of entities to return in a page.

page  int optional

Metadata about pagination.

GET Serie resource.

Get details of Serie model, find by slug of serie and slug of author.

Route name: api.v1.series.show

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/series/hobb-robin/les-aventuriers-de-la-mer-fr" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/series/hobb-robin/les-aventuriers-de-la-mer-fr"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://localhost:8000/api/v1/series/hobb-robin/les-aventuriers-de-la-mer-fr',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

Request      

GET api/v1/series/{author_slug}/{serie_slug}

URL Parameters

author_slug  string  

slug of author in meta.author series' list, in case of multiple authors, default author is selected so you need to refer to series' list and not authors' list, example: hobb-robin

serie_slug  string  

slug of serie in meta.slug series' list, example: les-aventuriers-de-la-mer-fr

GET Book collection of Serie.

Books list from one Serie, find by slug.

Route name: api.v1.series.show.books

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/series/books/taylor-dennis-e/nous-sommes-bob-fr?perPage=5&page=1" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/series/books/taylor-dennis-e/nous-sommes-bob-fr"
);

const params = {
    "perPage": "5",
    "page": "1",
};
Object.keys(params)
    .forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://localhost:8000/api/v1/series/books/taylor-dennis-e/nous-sommes-bob-fr',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
        'query' => [
            'perPage'=> '5',
            'page'=> '1',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

Request      

GET api/v1/series/books/{author_slug}/{serie_slug}

URL Parameters

author_slug  string  

slug of author in meta.author series' list, in case of multiple authors, default author is selected so you need to refer to series' list and not authors' list, example: taylor-dennis-e

serie_slug  string  

slug of serie in meta.slug series' list, example: nous-sommes-bob-fr

Query Parameters

perPage  int optional  

Number of entities to return in a page.

page  int optional  

Page number to return, 1 by default

GET Book collection of Serie (from volume).

Books list from one Serie, find by slug from volume and limited to 10 results.

Route name: api.v1.series.current

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/series/books/1/gemmell-david/drenai-fr" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/series/books/1/gemmell-david/drenai-fr"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://localhost:8000/api/v1/series/books/1/gemmell-david/drenai-fr',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));
